--
-- Table structure for table `tourplan`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `tourplan`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `tourplan` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `intro` text NOT NULL,
  `intro_main` text NOT NULL,
  `startDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `days` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `people` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `theme` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `reg_date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `edit_date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `member_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `likes` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `fk_tourPlan_member1_idx` (`member_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_tourPlan_member1` FOREIGN KEY (`member_id`) REFERENCES `member` (`member_id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=27 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;
